1b1(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga ta nit+ta gu h+ya dz+nyA na an+d+ra gar+b+hakra
1b2(rgyud): d+haku la tan tra bin thAr+tha bid+yA yog sid d+hi nA ma ma hA yan sU tra/ bod skad du/ de bzhin
1b3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs gsang ba'i ye shes don gyi snying po khro ba rdo rje'i rigs
1b4(rgyud): kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo rnal 'byor grub pa'i rgyud ces bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo// 
1b5(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das dpal sgrol byed thugs rje'i rgyal ba la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad
2a1(rgyud): bdag gis thos pI dus gcig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bcom ldan
2a2(rgyud): 'das dpal kun tu b.rang po rdo rje sbed he ru ka go sang ba mchog gi dge pa byin gyis brlabs kyi dbang phyug/ 
2a3(rgyud): mi zad mdzod kyi bkod pa/ che ba'i don lnga dam pa'i spyod pas bskyod pa de rmad du/ 
2a4(rgyud): gnas gsang ba'i yang gsang ba kun gzhi chos kyi dbyings kyi pho brang thig le bdel ba'i klong / ye 'byam rmad
2a5(rgyud): du grags pa'i gzhal yas rgya phyogs su yongs su mchod pa/ chos nyid kyi nam mkha' las cho 'phrul gyi sbyin
2a6(rgyud): kun du 'thibs pa/ byang chub kyi char mngon par 'bab pa/ nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba 'angs par gyur pa/ ye shes
2b1(rgyud): kyi b+ha gu mngon par bskyed pa/ mtha' da dbus med gra tse mo kun dun mnyam pa/ rin po cha'i rgyal pos rnam par brgyan pa/ mu tig gi lung mo dang / chun 'byung dang / wA kris
2b2(rgyud): mdzes pa/ nyi mchen bsngagasal btab pa/ rnang chen pos phra ba kod pa/ skar ma dang shin tu skar mdag gis gaper smras pa/ rdo rje rin po che'i 'di snang bas kun du mad
2b3(rgyud): ba'i mkhara' la/ rlung nag gi phung po rgya yongs su ma chad par mnyam pa/ khrag gi phung po dba' klang du 'khrug pa/ rgya phyogs su yongs su ma chad pa/ ma ting gi gnas dang / 
2b4(rgyud): 'brur 'brur chags pa/ rus pa phung po rgya kun du mnyam nga'i gzhi la 'bar ba'i gzhal yas/ kha bar kun tu 'phro ba/ ga pu cung brtsegs pa'i rtsig pa la/ gnam lcags kyi
2b5(rgyud): gzer tal bar btab pa/ rtsibs kun du nyi ma dang zla ba rangs pa dang ma rangs par 'byo ba/ nya chen po'i klu gdung la nya phran dral drab gtams pa/ zla bA'i ka rten dang / nyi ma'i ka l+r-i
2b6(rgyud): dang / sbrul chun gyi ka rgyan la sogasang / hU~M gi thig dang / me'i char mngon par 'bab pa/ chos nyid kyi blangs rnam par brgyad pa/ ye shes kyi lnga ldis mngon par bres pa/ 
2b7(rgyud): rgyan dang 'phen gyis klubs pa/ sbrul nag gri zer chags dang / sprin nag gi grib so lta bus gzhol bu'i bar bar thams cad na rin po che dang / mu tig dang / me tog gis mdzes
2b8(rgyud): pa/ 'khor ba'i maN+Dal yo bkra mal bam ril che chung dang / khog skam skad smad dang / yan lad ring thung dang / dbang po'i phreng ba dang / rdo rjes kun du spras pa/ sgo dgus kun
3a1(rgyud): du gsal bar gyur pa'i gnas na rdo rje rgyal chab ces bya ba'i zhe sdang rdo rje dang / rdo rje go 'ur zhes bya ba'i nga rgyal rin chen dang / rdo rje ging zhes bya
3a2(rgyud): 'dod chags pad mo dang / rdo rje karma zhes bya ba'i phrag dog sna tshogs dang / rdo rje bya rog ces bya ba'i drod kyi rtags 'dzin dang / rdo rje dus mtshams zhes bya ba'i 'thun 'jug gi
3a3(rgyud): bka' sdod dang / rdo rje spun thams cad dang / rdo rje ming thams cad dang / rdo rje rig 'dzin thams cad dang / rdo rje lus thams cad dang / rdo rje rnal 'byor thams cad dang / de rje/ 
3a4(rgyud): dag thams cad dang / rdo rje las thams cad dang / rdo rje yid thams cad dang / rdo rje ma thams cad dang / rdo rje ging thams cad dang / rdo rje na
3a5(rgyud): kyis 'gro ba thams cad dang / do phra men ma thams cad dang / rdo rje kun du 'bar ma thams cad dang / rdo rje gnid sbyin thams cad dang / rdo rje srin ma thams cad dang / rdo rje sras dang / 
3a6(rgyud): dang / bran mo la sogs pa bud med thams cad dang / rdo rje mngag pa la sogs pa'i rdo rje khro bo thams cad 'du bar gyur pa/ rdo rje rigs kyi sangs rgyas thams cad dang / 'gying bag
3a7(rgyud): tshul gyis bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar rdo rje'i gdan la 'khor mang po dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa ni 'di lta ste/ cha 'phrul chen po nam mkha' dbang phyug ces bya ba'i sangs
3a8(rgyud): sa dang / tsha 'phrul chen po rnam zla ba sbyin na mi bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / cha 'phrul chen po rnam grom sregs pa zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / tshe phrul chen pa thams cad
3b1(rgyud): grub pa zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / nam mkha'i bu mo dbang mo zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor mtshan mo dang / nam mkha'i bu mo dga' sdud ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / nam ma
3b2(rgyud): bu mo rnam par gdung mA zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / nam mkha'i bu mo sgrol ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor mchen mo la sogs te/ 
3b3(rgyud): yang dam tshig chen po'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ dam tshig chen po rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / dam tshid chen po nor bu'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / dam tshig
3b4(rgyud): po pad ma'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / dam tshig chen po bkod pa'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / dam tshig chen mo rdo rje dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor
3b5(rgyud): chen mo dang / dam tshig chen mo nor bu'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / dam tshig chen mo pad ma'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / dam
3b6(rgyud): chen mo rgyan gyi dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo la sogs te/ shin du mi 'da' ba chen po'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang tshad med pa'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ gsang
3b7(rgyud): bo byams pa'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / gasdang ba chen po snying rje'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / gsang ba chen po dga' ba'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas
3b8(rgyud): gsang ba chen po btang snyoms kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / gsang ba chen po bde ba'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor mchen mo dang / gsang ba chen
4a1(rgyud): 'joms byed dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / gsang ba chen mo dga' ba'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / gus
4a2(rgyud): ba chen mo khyab pa'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / shin du tshad med pa'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang rol pa chen po'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ rol pa chen po'i sa
4a3(rgyud): rgyas yak+Sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / ril pa chen po'i sangs rgya sa rak+Sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen po'i sang sa rgyas rtsig sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen po'i sangs
4a4(rgyud): rgyas be shwA hi ka zhes bya ba dang / ral ba chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma yAk+Sha shir ke zhes bya ba dang / ral pa chen mo'i rnal 'byed ma rak+Sha shor ka zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen mo'i rnal 'byo
4a5(rgyud): zlog sha shrI ri ki zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma bi shrI shor ki zhes bya ba dang / shin du rol pa chen po'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang 'jigs byed chun pa'i 'khor 'o
4a6(rgyud): khor sangs rgyas te sha he dro ka zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen po'i sangs rgyas ke sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen po'i sangs rgyas pa
4a7(rgyud): / zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen pa'i sangs rgyas pi shwa hi kau zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen ma'i rnal 'byor ma tri sha sha ri ke zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen ma'i rnal
4a8(rgyud): ma ke sha shor ke zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen ma'i rnal 'byor ma pe Ta sho ri ka zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma'i shwa sho ri ka zhes bya ba la lags pa shin tu
4b1(rgyud): 'jigs byed chen po'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang 'joms byed chen po'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ 'jams byed can pa'i sangs rgyas trag sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i sangs
4b2(rgyud): tri sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i sangs rgyas ka sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i sangs rgyas bag sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen mo'i rnal 'phye
4b3(rgyud): ba trag sha sho ra ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma tri shra she ri ka zhes bya ba dang / 'dzams byed chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma ka sha shoshau rA ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen mo
4b4(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma bag sha sher ka la sogs te/ shin du 'joms byed chen po'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang za byed chen pa' 'khor 'di lta ste/ babyed chen po'i sangs rgyas ru ti he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 
4b5(rgyud): dpa'i sangs rgyas rag ti he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen po'i sangs rgyas kha hi he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / zabyed chen po'i sangs rgyas sa ha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma
4b6(rgyud): sho ri ka zhes bya ba dang / byed chen ma'i rnal 'byor ma rag te sho ri ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen ma'i rnal 'byor ma kha hi sha ri ka zhes bya ba dang / ba byed chen ma'i rnal 'byor ma sa ha sho rI ka zhes bya
4b7(rgyud): la sogs pa rnal 'byor mi'i 'khor rab tu mang zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i he ru ka mtha' yas pa sha stag rnams dang / gzhan yong gsang ba'i bu ma 'khor 'di lta ste/ gsang ba'i bu mod
4b8(rgyud): mo zhes bya ba dang / gsang ba'i bu mo rkun mo zhes bya ba dang / gsang ba'i bu mo rmongs mo nas bya ba dang / gsang ba'i bu mor langs ma zhes bya ba dang / gsang ba'i bu mo lbos mo zhes bya ba dang / 
5a1(rgyud): gsang ba'i bu mo gtum mo zhes bya ba dang / gsang ba'i bu mo swa shan+dan zhes bya ba dang / gsang ba'i bu mo mtshogs ma zhes bya ba la sogs pa shin tu gsang ba'i bu mo'i 'tsha
5a2(rgyud): bsam kyis mi khyab pa dang / gzhan yang dga' ba'i bu mo'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ dga' ba'i bu mo seng gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / dga' ba'i bu mo bya rgod
5a3(rgyud): stag gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / dga' ba'i bu mo la gdang ma zhes bya ba dang / dga' ba'i bu mo byi gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / dga' ba'i bu mo dur bya'i gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / dga' ba'i bu mo khA gdong
5a4(rgyud): ma zhes bya ba dang / dga' ba'i bu ma mun gdong ma zhes bya ba la sogs pa shin tu dga' bde bu mo'i 'khor ba pam gyis mi khyab pa dang / gzhan yang shin tu gus pa'i bu mo'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ 
5a5(rgyud): tu gus pa'i bu mo rta gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gus pa'i bu mo phag gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gus pa'i bu mo spre'u gdong ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gus pa'i bu mo bral bya
5a6(rgyud): sogs pa shin tu gus pa'i bu ma'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang shin tu gsad pa chen po'i sras kyi 'kho la 'di lta ste/ shin tu ga sa pa chen po dpal stag gi ma grin+da zhes bya ba dang / shinatu
5a7(rgyud): gsod pa chen po dpal g.yag gi mgrin zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod pa chen po dpal sha ba'i mgrin zhes bya ba dang / 
5a8(rgyud): drugs pa chen po da pa la rta'i mgrin zhes byab / shin tug sad pa chen po dpal myung gu'i mgrin zhes bya ba dang / shin tugs pa chen po dpa la sa ga'i mgrin zhes bya ba dang / shin tugs
5b1(rgyud): ban po da la dom gyi ma dran zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod pa chen po dpa pa phag gi mgrin zhes bya dang / shin tu gas chen pa da la dred mo'i mgrin zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsad
5b2(rgyud): rdo rje gsod ma zhes byung dang / shin tu gas dam chen mor dung khrod ces bya ba dang / shin tu gasrad mchen ma rdo rje gtun khung zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod mtshan ma rdo rje gtum mo zhes byar
5b3(rgyud): dang / shin tu gsod ma chen mo rdo rje mda' snyems ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod ma chen po rdo rje smra 'byin ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod ma chen mo rdo rje za byed ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gas
5b4(rgyud): chen mo rje dred ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod mtshan mo rdo rje spor ma zhes bya ba dang / shin tu gsod ma chen mi'i 'khar rab tu mang po rnams dang / de dag la sogs te rdul phra rab snyed dang 'ang
5b5(rgyud): cig go/ yum rdo rje kun tu bzang mo sang sho ri kas kyang nyid kyi sku la rnam par 'khril te/ mdun gyis bltas nas thabs gcig go// de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po des
5b6(rgyud): chos thams cad dgongs pa mnyam pa nyid la shar bar mkhyen nas sku mnyam pa nyid mi dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i ngang la snyoms par zhugs so// gsung mnyam pa nyid mi dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i
5b7(rgyud): rnam par zhugs so// thugs mnyam pa nyid mi dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i dang la rnam par bzhugs te/ 'jug pa 'am/ ldog pa'am/ rnam par ldogang mi dmigs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das
5b8(rgyud): gsang ba mchag gi bdag po des dbyings kyi dang la mi g.yo ba mnakha 'azhin du yumado ji kud thab rang mas snang pa nyid kyi gru 'di blangs te rnam par 'askul to// yod med stong pa shin tu nal
6a1(rgyud): 'byar mthus// nam mkha' bzhin las dam tshig nye bar gshegs// ye shes rgya mtsho rnam par grol ba'i klong // mi gnas mi dmigs nam mkha'i dbyings nas
6a2(rgyud): bzhengs// zhes bskul nas/ bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i mchog gi bdag po des chos thams cad byang chub sems la shar bar mkhyen nas stong pa nyid kyi dang las rdo rje'i sku mngon
6a3(rgyud): dper na nam mkha' dang pa las zla ba dri ma med pa shar ba lta bu'o// de nas yum sang shor ka la gzigs te/ 'dzum pa rnam par mdzad do// dper na nyi ma stong las 'od kyi zer ba
6a4(rgyud): dzu'o// de nas 'od kyi zer de dag las byang chub kyi sprin mngon par 'khrigs te/ rol pa'i char mngon par phab pas rol pa sna tshogs kyi 'brug dang / ral pa sna tshogs kyi glog dang / 
6a5(rgyud): sna tshogs kyi mchod pa dang rol pa sna tshogs kyi glu dang ral pas tshogs kyi gar dang / rol pa sna tshogs kyi rnga dang / dung dang ker kor dang gling bu dang ral pa sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang / rol ba snga
6a6(rgyud): kyi sreg pa dang sdig pa dang / lakhyud pa dang steng pa dang / sbyor ba ding bstim pa dang mnyes pa dang / rol pas chags kyis gsol ba dang myang ba dang / 'chal ba dang bde ba dang / spong dang
6a7(rgyud): dang / 'jug pa dang / rol pa sna tshogs kyi dga' ba chen po la 'jug pa rnam par mdzad do// de nas lu dun tu bzang mdes spyan rim bkra kes rnam par 'dud pa'i tshul du bcom ldan 'ad
6a8(rgyud): sangang mchog gi bdag po la rnam par bltas te/ rnal 'byor sbyor ba'i phyag lus kun tu se la brdabs nas rol pa chen po'i glu 'dis gsol ba btab bo// tshogs chen gnyis
6b1(rgyud): thugs dam dbyings kyi d+ha/ padza rol pa chen po'i sku// rdo rje sems dpa' skal bzang pal khyod bdag/ thabs kyi rol pas bde chen dbyings nas bzhengs// de nas
6b2(rgyud): tsam ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gis bdag po das glu des bsngal bar thugs su chud nas/ bde ba chen po'i dang de las cho 'phrul chen por rnam par bzhengs te/ rnam par 'gying ba dang / rna
6b3(rgyud): par brjid pa dang / gar gyi phyag rgya chen po dang / rnam par bshad pa sna tshogs dang / zhabs kyi brkyang bskum dang / skra'i 'gyur bag dang / smin ris kyi 'bri kuta bsgyur ba dang / sprul pa'i 'od
6b4(rgyud): nam mkha' thams cad kun du khyab par mdzad do// de nas thams cad dang thams cad la mtshan ma dang / rnam pa dang / yod pa dang / med pa thams cad la gsang ba mchog gi bdag po des kun la
6b5(rgyud): khyab par ma de/ de dag gi rang bzhin du rnam par gnas so// de nas da nga kun tu pa rang mad mtshar du gyur te/ yang rnam 'byengar ba'i phyag lus kun du stsal brdabs te/ tsha 'phrul 'byung ba'i grwa
6b6(rgyud): 'dis gsol ba btab bo// ye shes snrums rnam par rol pa'i sku// thabs dang shes rab che la mda' brnyas pa'i// 'phags rje sprul pa mang po 'byung ba'i gnas// bde gshegs pa dngar
6b7(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gis bdag po des rdo rje rol pa'i dri kho na nyid ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas cang mI gsung
6b8(rgyud): rabazhugs so// de nas yum rdo rje kun du bzang mo dang / dam tshig chen po rdo rje sems dpa' la sogs pa 'khor shin tu mang po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur te/ de dag thams cad mgrin gcig
7a1(rgyud): rdo rje ral pa de kha na'i glu 'das bskul te gsol ba btab po// e ma'o// yid bzhin sku mchog nam mkha' lta bu las// khyab pa'i byin brlabs rdo rje gar mdza
7a2(rgyud): cing // gzi brjid smin dpung rol pas bsgyings pa'i sku// zags med rdo rje ral pa'i cho 'phrul ston// e ma'o// yid bzhin gsung mchog sgra brnyan lta bu las// sman pa'i byin brlabs
7a3(rgyud): // yan lag rga mtshom zad bkad pa'i gsung // seng ge skra yis gsang sngags rgya mtsho ston// e ma'o/ ye shes snying po nyi ma lta bu las// ye shes byin brlabs
7a4(rgyud): bde mdzad cing // thig le skyes bral rnam par mi rtag zugs// rnam grol de nyid nges pa'i cho 'phrul sngon// mi shes blan mongs 'dam bying 'gro ba rnams// sdug bsngal rgya mtshos bcings pa
7a5(rgyud): bas kyis khral// ma rig mun pas ldongs pa don gyis phye/ 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho rol pa'i gru yis sgrol// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi thugs chen po// ye shes don gyi snying po mchog dang
7a6(rgyud): ldar// rnal 'byor theg chen de rje kun 'das rgyud// 'das de'i tshogs la rgya cher bshad du gsol// a la la ha zhes nges par btud de gsal ba btar po// de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang
7a7(rgyud): rol pade kho na nyid kyi phu de sA gsol ba btab pa mkhyen nas 'khor thams cad la rnam par gzegs te 'dzum pa mdzad do// 'dzum pa mdzad pa' thugs rnam
7a8(rgyud): bar dag pa'i klong nas rig pa'i nyi ma brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang mi lang ba'i 'od zer dang bcas pa 'byam klas pa khyab par shar bar mdzad do// 'od zer de dag ri re las da rje he ru ka rab tu ma
7b1(rgyud): nga'i tshogs bshad par mdzad do// de dag re re las kyang sangs rgyas 'bum phrag 'khor sa so'o zha'as 'bring bcas pa ldan gyis grub par mdzad do// de dag las rig pa'i nyi ma'i char ma
7b2(rgyud): par 'babs mun pa'i klong thams cad gsal bar mdzad do// rig pa'i chos kyi 'brug sgra dang / rig pa'i chos kyi char dang / rig pa'i chos kyi klu sna tshogs dang / glar sna tshogs dang / rig pa
7b3(rgyud): chos kyi mchod pa sna tshogs byang ste/ 'byam klas pa'i nam mkha' la sgra sna tshogs phan tshun dang / yan man dang / snrel zhi la sogs pa thams cad du khyab par ling long pyad par byung ngo // 
7b4(rgyud): mchod pa'i char yang mngon par phab/ rmad du byung ba'i sku bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang ling long pyad rmad du byung ba'i thugs kyang lgang nga'o// rmad du byeng ba'i gsung bsam gyis mi khyab pa
7b5(rgyud): yang a la la ho zhes sgra sogs/ sangs rgyas 'bum phrag kyang gsung dbyangs bsdam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgra gcig tu/ e ma'o rmad byang rol pa'i chos kyi don byung ngo zhes sgrogs/ 
7b6(rgyud): 'bul phrag dang gdul bya sna tshogs spro ba'i ngo mtshar skyed/ reg pa'i rgyal sbyangs don gyi che ba phyung / rim zhing ngo mtshar bar gyur te thams cad nye bar gnas so// de na sde yang bcom ldan 'das
7b7(rgyud): kasang ba mchog gi bdag po des 'khor rnam par spyod pa'i rdo rje rgyun zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje sngags kyi tshig 'dis gsungs
